I immediately received a text from their manager to wait and come in when staff is available, which is M-F during normal working hours.

So, ok, I arrived on Monday about Noonish, the manager was on break so one of the receptionist assisted me but not before telling me that I needed to wear a mask because this Anytime Fitness is connected to a physical therapy center with some elderly people, regular folks and ppl being "worked on" at the massage tables, themselves wearing their masks.
She said something about, if other people see me Not wearing a mask it may cause some kind of a potential hazard to the others? (I'm thinking,,, What hazard, what risks?üôÑ)
She took my temperature, I said that I'm healthy and that if sick people who are scared of getting Covid-19 shouldn't be out anyways for their own protection, right? And that I have a medical condition, which requires me to breath in fresh air,,, especially if I'm working out or gonna be exerting myself, duh (common sense). It's imperative that our body, mind and overall complete system get enough air fresh to be naturally rejuvenated and heal for soul-mind-body wellness.

The receptionist was cool about it and seem to understand the logic, wanting to remedy this situation, she suggested that I come back after hours when the physical therapy center was close but the gym remains open? I couldn't do that, telling her that I was instructed to come check in during working hours being that it was my first day and that I was given instructions to come between those hours. (Plus, I was already there,, why the inconvenience of coming back later on at night, wasting more fuel, time and causing unnecessary trouble.)üôÑ

As I was putting on my mask in the waiting room she kindly allowed me to go work out until the Anytime Fitness manager was back from break in order to check me in officially. After about 45 minutes of stretching, leg presses, lower back workouts a shorter, round woman comes out to inform me that I was granted only this 1 visit and Not the 7 day promotion like other people were getting (which was their advertisement & promotion). She informed me that it was her that texted me to let me know to come in during normal working hours BUT she didn't informed by text that it was only a 1 time visit. üôÑüò¥

It's a 25 mile rd trip for me with congested traffick, it took me 45 minutes just to drive there and back home (60 & 91 FW üôÑ). She could have saved me the time, the trouble by letting me know of the 1 day & not the 7 days. For me, I wouldn't make this drive or the hassle involved if it was for 1, 45 minute workout.

I think it's their hidden prejudice and fears.
My physical appearance could have intimated or triggered them? (I'm not an old white woman needing their therapy session. I'm there to exercise and maintain fitness.)
I was wearing a mask during my workouts but it would slide below my nose periodically when I needed to breath after each set and not suffocate or causing harmüôÑ. I workout away from others, wiped down equipments, had my ear buds on, doing my own thing without interference.
The manager didn't explain a whole lot and seemed to just want me out of there asap.

I think they came together with the manager & made a judgement call. I think they came to their own conclusions and made their call without really hearing me out and understanding the real facts about Covid. (Is it 1, 2 or 3 masks, 6 feet apart and with Vaccinations? And, what are you scared of? Aren't you immune after your Vaxxs?)üôÑ

I had to cut my workout short after one of their male therapist (a short, semi bald slightly overweight fellow comes over to me,,, inches away from my face and Not 6 feet away as is their policy,,, to tell me to put my mask back up. I ignored him, finished my last set, grab my things.

By this time, it was already getting too much. Getting cold & angry looks from their employees & therapists under their masks üò∑. I left.< /Review></record>

< review>
I made a yelp account just for this review.
Story time:
A year ago I went to a previous mechanic in Escondido who charged $300 for a fuel pump. Few months later, went to RMW for a transmission sensor, they charged $600. Was handled quickly, didn't second-guess it. 1 week ago, my ride overheats and shuts down. Ramona Motor Works tells me I have leaks in my coolant and my radiator, quotes me at $1100. Still clueless at this time, I say ok. They call back next day to tell me they "ran a second test, and it did not pass that test" (no specifics). But I was told my head gasket was blown and it would cost up to an additional $4k. Thought this was sketchy and researched my previous repairs. A fuel pump with parts and labor runs between $250 and $1000, meaning the first mechanic in Escondido was honest. Can't say the same about RMW. A transmission sensor goes for $10 to $100, with $80 to $100 for labor... $200 tops. Even with an additional $100 added, they still charged double what they should have. Drove my overheated van to Escondido to the previous mechanic, he plugged leaks in the in the coolant hose/tank, no more overheating. Radiator was fine, no issues found with head gasket. Took him 3 hours (including letting the van run for 2 hours for tests). These people at Ramona Motor Works overcharge and price gouge during a pandemic and prey on those not savvy on vehicles. I see them as a chop shop now and will not be returning. I do not trust anything about this business down to the reviews on their Google page. If your vehicle breaks down and you want to save money, pay to tow it to an honest mechanic in Escondido (I recommend On Schedule). If you have deep pockets and don't care about money, they'll be happy to help in a timely fashion... 1 star.< /review>

< Review>
I spent some time at the nursery and loved it! There were so many plants of different sizes and varieties, and plants I didn't know existed.   Many of them I've seen used for landscaping in the community.  Robert & the team are an encyclopedia of information on everything in that nursery.  The people here are the kindness, most down-to-earth souls you'll ever meet.  One of the first and most interesting things I learned was that as a wholesaler, their goal isn't to provide the kind of customer service you'd expect to get at Home Depot.  The employees do their best to point customers in the right direction, but their focus is to keep the plants thriving, receiving new plants, and preparing large orders, among many other things needed to keep a nursery running.  Show up knowing what you're looking for or be OK to explore on your own, and when you have a question someone will be happy to help you out.<//Review>

<response>None< /response>< Review>
They have the best selection California Native plants. They have more variety of natives than any other place in the local area.
However, do not expect ANY help from the staff regarding suggested plants for your yard/ or tips. The plants do not have a price tag. It is a cumbersome process of going to every plant you like with a pen-paper, noting size and description, then to the front desk, then wait patiently till the staff thinks you are important enough to be helped. Once you know the rate and decided on which plans to buy (you are mostly lost at this point because you have forgotten which plant looked like what and where was it located in the nursery. Then back to finding your plant, lugging it to the checkout (they have some carts, but no help). Then pay and load. Uff! They seem to want to only cater to experts/ bulk buyers who know exactly what they want, just pay and go. Unlike hobbyist who ask several questions.
Recommended for their collection and price, but not for a beginner plant enthusiast who needs any kind of help.<//Review>

<Rating>4</Rating><Text>April 2021. This location is only accessible through a small park that is apparently gated and locked up most of the time per other reviews.

There's virtually no parking in the immediate neighborhood unless you're a resident.

To my surprise, when I got there the gate was open - so I was able to park in the small parking lot.

This is a beautiful spot with clay banks by the river. There are some trails into the wooded area away from the houses overlooking the river. When I was there there were two young guys collecting garbage and hauling it out - which was great to see!< /Text>< pics>

< review>
I would not recommend C&C Property to any potential renter. Save your money, time, and energy. It is in your best interest to read other reviews as most of us potential renters have encountered the same issues.

C&C process for potential renters is to submit an application ($25 fee per applicant) and within the three month period, apply up to 6 rentals. Example, if you apply to a unit and the lease goes to another tenant, you are eligible to transfer your application to another unit that is available for rent and not have to pay the application fee again.

I have applied to three different units within C&C and the process has been similar to pulling teeth. No one in the office has been good at communication or advising why my applications have not been accepted. I have emailed Mel Lagrama several times for additional support only to have my emails and calls unanswered. I‚Äôve asked to speak with Mel‚Äôs supervisor for additional support and of course, radio silence. I have yet to hear back from C&C.

The customer service team that answers the phones are not additionally informed about the rental properties listed. When you call for more information about a unit (which is stated to do so on their website) they only have access to what is already listed on their website. The phone answering customer service team has little to no information to guide you.

Additionally, the rental postings do not have all needed information such as square footage, laundry situation, outdoor space, etc. I‚Äôm not clear on why they do not require this information from properties before posting. A lot of the info and pictures are quite minimal and then have a customer service team who knows no better, makes it frustrating. Who is the subject matter expert and where are they hiding?

I have asked for a refund for my application fee and while they are very quick to advise that it is NOT company policy to provide refunds,  when asked what their company policy is on assisting potential tenants/renters, there is no answer.

Three weeks in and I still cannot get anyone to contact me back but my money was taken quite quickly.

If you‚Äôve read this far, thank you. My experience with C&C has just been the worst and with moving already being a stressful and expensive process, they have done their very best at being a waste of good time and money. Never again.< /review>

I showed up a day early by accident and they fit me in their schedule with only a very short wait.  The place was clean and organized.  The technician and radiologist were nice and compassionate.  5 stars for patient care.

Now the bad.  Prior to making my appointment I called to obtain a quote as I knew I had not yet met my deductible for the year and I knew that where I had gone in the past was very expensive.  I was given a quote and I even asked her to double check the amount as the quote was significantly less than my prior place.  I received the invoice - for 40% more than what I had been quoted.  I called to discuss the issue and was told that the quote I had been given was only an estimate and I needed to take it up with my insurance company as that is who my dispute is with.  I told them no, my dispute is with them as they were the ones that gave me the quote and I was not told it was an estimate. I had an appointment scheduled for an MRI with the San Clemente Memorial Care Imaging Center for Friday, November 29th.
